function v_u_1.CaseInfo(p7) -- name: CaseInfo
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_5
	local v8, v9 = v_u_1.CustomCase(p7)
	local v10 = {}
	for v11, v12 in v8 do
		table.insert(v10, { v11, v12 })
	end
	table.sort(p7, function(p13, p14)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5
		return v_u_5.Gifts[p13].Price > v_u_5.Gifts[p14].Price
	end)
	return {
		["Price"] = nil,
		["Image"] = "126118629758124",
		["Drop"] = nil,
		["Custom"] = true,
		["Top3"] = nil,
		["Price"] = v9,
		["Drop"] = v10,
		["Top3"] = { p7[1], p7[2], p7[3] }
	}
end
function v_u_1.CustomCase(p15) -- name: CustomCase
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_1
	local v16 = (1 / 0)
	local v17 = {}
	local v18 = 0
	local v19 = {}
	local v20 = ""
	for _, v21 in p15 do
		local v22 = v_u_5.Gifts[v21]
		if v22.Price < v16 then
			v16 = v22.Price
			v20 = v21
		end
	end
	for _, v23 in p15 do
		local v24 = 1 / (v_u_5.Gifts[v23].Price / v16)
		v17[v23] = v24
		v18 = v18 + v24
	end
	for _, v25 in p15 do
		local v26 = v17[v25] / v18 * 100000
		local v27 = math.round(v26) / 1000
		local _ = v17[v25] / v18 * 100
		v19[v25] = v27
	end
	local v28 = 0
	for _, v29 in p15 do
		local v30 = (v28 + v19[v29]) * 1000
		v28 = math.round(v30) / 1000
	end
	local v31 = 100 - v28
	v19[v20] = v19[v20] + v31
	local v32 = 0
	local v33 = 0
	for _, v34 in p15 do
		v32 = v32 + v19[v34] / 100 * v_u_5.Gifts[v34].Price
		local v35 = (v33 + v19[v34]) * 1000
		v33 = math.round(v35) / 1000
	end
	local v36 = v_u_1.GetROI1(v32)
	local v37 = math.round(v32) / v36 / 5
	return v19, math.round(v37) * 5
end
function v_u_1.GetROI1(p38) -- name: GetROI1
	local v39 = math.min(500000000, p38)
	return (math.max(2000000, v39) - 2000000) / 498000000 * -0.25 + 0.85
end
function v_u_1.GetROI(p40) -- name: GetROI
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5
	local v_u_41 = v_u_5.Cases[p40].Drop
	local v_u_42 = v_u_5.Cases[p40].Price
	table.sort(v_u_41, function(p43, p44)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_5
		return v_u_5.Gifts[p43[1]].Price < v_u_5.Gifts[p44[1]].Price
	end)
	local function v50(p45) -- name: E
		-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_41, (ref) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_42
		local v46 = 0
		local v47 = 0
		for v48 = 1, #v_u_41 do
			local v49 = v_u_41[v48][2] / 100
			v47 = v47 + ((v46 + v49) ^ p45 - v46 ^ p45) * v_u_5.Gifts[v_u_41[v48][1]].Price
			v46 = v46 + v49
		end
		return v47 / v_u_42
	end
	return v50(1), v50(2), v50(4)
end
function v_u_1.GroupTransparency(p51, p52, p53) -- name: GroupTransparency
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2
	local v54 = p51:GetDescendants()
	table.insert(v54, p51)
	for _, v55 in v54 do
		if v55:IsA("TextLabel") then
			if p53 then
				v_u_2:Create(v55, TweenInfo.new(p53), {
					["TextTransparency"] = p52
				}):Play()
			else
				v55.TextTransparency = p52
			end
		elseif v55:IsA("ImageLabel") then
			if p53 then
				v_u_2:Create(v55, TweenInfo.new(p53), {
					["ImageTransparency"] = p52
				}):Play()
			else
				v55.ImageTransparency = p52
			end
		end
		if v55:IsA("GuiObject") then
			if p53 then
				v_u_2:Create(v55, TweenInfo.new(p53), {
					["BackgroundTransparency"] = p52
				}):Play()
			else
				v55.BackgroundTransparency = p52
			end
		end
	end
end
function v_u_1.SimpleNumber(p56) -- name: SimpleNumber
	local v57 = math.floor(p56)
	local v58 = tostring(v57)
	repeat
		local v59
		v58, v59 = string.gsub(v58, "^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2")
	until v59 == 0
	return v58
end
function v_u_1.CreateSound(p60, p61) -- name: CreateSound
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	if not (p61 and (p61:IsA("Frame") or p61:IsA("ScrollingFrame"))) or p61.Visible then
		local v62 = p60:Clone()
		v62.Parent = p61 or v_u_6.PlayerGui
		v62:Play()
		game.Debris:AddItem(v62, v62.TimeLength)
		return v62
	end
end
function v_u_1.CreatePitchSound(p63, p64, p65) -- name: CreatePitchSound
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6
	if not (p65 and (p65:IsA("Frame") or p65:IsA("ScrollingFrame"))) or p65.Visible then
		local v66 = p63:Clone()
		v66.Parent = p65 or v_u_6.PlayerGui
		local v67 = Instance.new("PitchShiftSoundEffect")
		v67.Parent = v66
		v67.Octave = p64
		v66:Play()
		game.Debris:AddItem(v66, v66.TimeLength)
		return v66
	end
end
function v_u_1.Notify(p68, p69, p70) -- name: Notify
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_3
	if p70 then
		v_u_1.CreateSound(p70)
	end
	v_u_3:SetCore("SendNotification", {
		["Title"] = p68,
		["Text"] = p69
	})
end
function v_u_1.SortedGifts() -- name: SortedGifts
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5
	local v71 = {}
	for v72, v73 in v_u_5.Gifts do
		local v74 = table.clone(v73)
		v74.Name = v72
		table.insert(v71, v74)
	end
	table.sort(v71, function(p75, p76)
		return p75.Price < p76.Price
	end)
	local v77 = {}
	for _, v78 in v71 do
		local v79 = v78.Name
		table.insert(v77, v79)
	end
	return v77
end
return v_u_1

function handleDescendant(p8) -- name: handleDescendant
	if p8.Name ~= "Profile" or p8.Parent.Name ~= "Right" then
		if p8:IsA("TextButton") or p8:IsA("ImageButton") then
			if p8:GetAttribute("DONT_ANIMATE") then
				return
			end
			local v9
			if p8:FindFirstChild("Container") then
				v9 = p8.Container
			else
				v9 = p8
			end
			local v_u_10, v_u_11 = getTweens(v9)
			local v_u_12 = false
			p8.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_10
				if not v_u_12 then
					v_u_12 = true
					v_u_10:Play()
				end
			end)
			p8.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
				v_u_12 = false
				v_u_11:Play()
			end)
			p8.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_12, (copy) v_u_11
				v_u_12 = false
				v_u_11:Play()
			end)
		end
	end
end

local function v_u_36() -- name: updateXP
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_11, (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_14
	local v24 = v_u_11.Frame.Level.Progress.LevelNum
	local v25 = v_u_13.Value
	v24.Text = tostring(v25)
	local v26 = v_u_11.Frame.Level.Progress.Percentage
	local v27 = v_u_14.Value
	local v28 = v_u_13.Value + 1
	local v29
	if v28 <= 25 then
		v29 = v28 * 100 + 200
	else
		v29 = v28 * 160 + 500
	end
	v26.Value = v27 / v29 * 100
	local v30 = v_u_11.Frame.Level.xp
	local v31 = v_u_14.Value
	local v32 = tostring(v31)
	local v33 = "/<font color=\'#7f7f7f\'>"
	local v34 = v_u_13.Value + 1
	local v35
	if v34 <= 25 then
		v35 = v34 * 100 + 200
	else
		v35 = v34 * 160 + 500
	end
	v30.Text = v32 .. v33 .. tostring(v35) .. "</font>"
end
local function v_u_44(p37, p38, p39) -- name: updateStatus
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_13
	local v40 = p37.Status
	local v41 = tostring(p38) .. (p39 and "Prem" or "Free")
	local v42 = v_u_16:FindFirstChild(v41)
	if not v42 then
		v42 = Instance.new("BoolValue")
		v42.Name = v41
		v42.Value = false
		v42.Parent = v_u_16
	end
	local v43 = v_u_15.Value == 1
	if p39 then
		if v43 then
			if p38 < v_u_13.Value then
				v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
				return
			elseif p38 == v_u_13.Value then
				v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
			else
				v40.Image = "rbxassetid://105706361949544"
			end
		else
			v40.Image = "rbxassetid://105706361949544"
			return
		end
	elseif p38 < v_u_13.Value then
		v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
		return
	elseif p38 == v_u_13.Value then
		v40.Image = v42.Value and "rbxassetid://84426118156719" or "rbxassetid://102794832629735"
	else
		v40.Image = "rbxassetid://105706361949544"
	end
end
local function v_u_54(p45, p46) -- name: updateXPBar
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_17
	if p46 <= v_u_13.Value then
		p45.XPBar.Visible = true
		p45.XPBar.Progress.Fill.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		p45.XPBar.Level.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(55, 100, 221)
		p45.LockedXPBar.Visible = false
		return
	elseif p46 == v_u_13.Value + 1 then

local function v_u_107(p101) -- name: formatReward
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8
	local v102
	if p101[1] == "snow" then
		v102 = "Snowflakes"
	elseif p101[1] == "gems" then
		v102 = "Gems"
	elseif p101[1] == "ton" then
		v102 = "TON"
	elseif p101[1] == "stars" then
		v102 = "Stars"
	elseif p101[1] == "x2" then
		v102 = "x2 Luck Potion"
	elseif p101[1] == "x4" then
		v102 = "x4 Luck Potion"
	else
		local v103 = p101[2]
		v102 = tostring(v103)
	end
	if p101[1] == "x2" or p101[1] == "x4" then
		local v104 = p101[2] or 1
		return v102 .. " (" .. tostring(v104) .. "sec)", "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_5.Icons[p101[1]]
	end
	if p101[1] == "item" then
		return v102, "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[p101[2]].Image
	end
	if p101[2] then
		local v105 = v_u_8.SimpleNumber
		local v106 = p101[2]
		v102 = v102 .. " (x" .. tostring(v105(v106)) .. ")"
	end
	return v102, "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_5.Icons[p101[1]]
end

local function v_u_141() -- name: update
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_131, (copy) v_u_11
	local v132 = v_u_131 - os.time()
	if v132 <= 432000 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 48, 51)
	elseif v132 <= 0 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = "Ended!"
		return
	end
	local v133 = v132 / 86400
	local v134 = math.floor(v133)
	local v135 = v132 % 86400 / 3600
	local v136 = math.floor(v135)
	local v137 = v132 % 3600 / 60
	local v138 = math.floor(v137)
	local v139 = v132 % 60
	local v140 = math.floor(v139)
	v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = string.format("Ends in: %02d:%02d:%02d:%02d", v134, v136, v138, v140)
	if v132 <= 0 then
		v_u_11.Frame.Timer.TextLabel.Text = "Ended!"
	end
end

	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_3

v_u_9.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_4, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_14
	local v15 = 0
	for _, v16 in v_u_10 do
		v15 = v15 + v16
	end
	if v15 > 10 or v15 < 1 then
		return
	else
		local v17 = {}
		for v18, v19 in v_u_10 do
			for _ = 1, v19 do
				table.insert(v17, v18)
			end
		end
		if #v17 > 10 or #v17 < 1 then
			return
		else
			local v20, v21 = v_u_4.Battles:InvokeServer("Create", v17, {})
			if v20 then
				v_u_7.MainFrame.Visible = false
				v_u_6.Visible = false
				v_u_7:WaitForChild("Battle").Visible = true
				v_u_10 = {}
				for _, v22 in v_u_8:GetChildren() do
					if v22:IsA("Frame") and v22:FindFirstChild("Buttons") then
						v22.Buttons.Selected.Visible = false
					end
				end
				v_u_14()
				v_u_4.Btl:Fire(v17)
			else
				v_u_3.Notify("ERROR", v21, v_u_5.UI_Error)
			end
		end
	end
end)

local function v_u_25() -- name: GetResultTable
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_6
	local v24 = {
		["FullName"] = v_u_21[2],
		["NFT"] = string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[1]
	}
	if string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[2] then
		v24.Model = string.split(string.split(v_u_21[2], " (")[2], ")")[1]
	else
		v24.Model = "Default"
	end
	v24.Owner = v_u_21[3]
	v24.Backdrop = v_u_21[4]
	v24.Color = v_u_6.Backdrops[v_u_21[4]]
	v24.Pattern = v_u_21[5]
	v24.Date = v_u_21[6]
	v24.Number = v_u_21[7]
	return v24
end
local function v_u_33(p26) -- name: radialprogress
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_5
	local v27 = p26 / 100 * 360
	local v28 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.Left.Circle
	local v29 = v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.Right.Circle
	if p26 > 0 and p26 <= 50 then
		v29.Visible = false
		v28.Visible = true
		v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180 + v27
		}):Play()
		return
	elseif p26 <= 0 then
		if v29.UIGradient.Rotation ~= -180 then
			local v30 = v_u_5:Create(v29.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
				["Rotation"] = -180
			})
			v30:Play()
			v30.Completed:Wait()
		end
		local v31 = v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180
		})
		v31:Play()
		v31.Completed:Wait()
		v29.Visible = false
		v28.Visible = false
	else
		v28.Visible = true
		v29.Visible = true
		local v32 = v_u_5:Create(v28.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = 0
		})
		v32:Play()
		v32.Completed:Wait()
		v_u_5:Create(v29.UIGradient, TweenInfo.new(0.25, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Rotation"] = -180 + (v27 - 180)
		}):Play()
	end
end
local function v_u_43() -- name: UpdateSelected
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_14, (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_33
	local v34 = 0
	local v35 = ""
	for v36 = 1, 4 do
		local v37 = v_u_10:FindFirstChild("Frame" .. v36)
		if v_u_16[v36] then
			v37.NFTFrame.NFT.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_16[v36].Name].Image
			for _, v38 in v37.NFTFrame.Patterns:GetChildren() do
				v38.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_14[v_u_16[v36]:GetAttribute("Pattern")]
			end
			v37.NFTFrame.BackgroundColor3 = v_u_6.Backdrops[v_u_16[v36]:GetAttribute("Backdrop")]
			local v39 = (v_u_6.Gifts[v_u_16[v36].Name].Price or 0) / 320000000
			local v40 = math.clamp(v39, 0, 1) * 20 + 5
			local v41 = math.round(v40)
			v34 = v34 + v41
			v37.NFTFrame.Percent.Text = tostring(v41) .. "%"
			v37.NFTFrame.Visible = true
			v35 = string.split(v_u_16[v36].Name, " (")[1]
		else
			v37.NFTFrame.Visible = false
		end
	end
	if #v_u_16 <= 0 then
		v_u_22 = nil
		v35 = ""
	end
	local v42 = math.clamp(v34, 0, 100)
	task.spawn(v_u_33, v42)
	v_u_10.FinalFrame.Frame.percent.Text = tostring(v42) .. "%"
	v_u_10.Button.Succ.Text = "Success Chance: " .. tostring(v42) .. "%"
	if v_u_22 then
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft " .. v35 .. " " .. v_u_22
	else
		v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft"
	end
end
local function v_u_46(p44) -- name: SelectGift
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_43
	if not table.find(v_u_16, p44) then
		if v_u_16[1] then
			if string.split(v_u_16[1].Name, " (")[1] == string.split(p44.Name, " (")[1] then
				if #v_u_16 < 4 then
					local v45 = v_u_16
					table.insert(v45, p44)
				end
			else
				v_u_16 = { p44 }
				v_u_22 = string.split(p44:GetAttribute("Number"), " ")[2]
			end
		else
			v_u_16 = { p44 }
			v_u_22 = string.split(p44:GetAttribute("Number"), " ")[2]
		end
		v_u_43()
	end
end

	v_u_43()
	if p47[1] == "Failed" then
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.hammer.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.anvil.Visible = false
		v_u_10.FinalFrame.broken.Visible = true

		v_u_10.FinalFrame.broken.Visible = false

		v_u_10.Button.Succ.Visible = false
		v_u_17 = false
		v_u_3.CreateSound(v_u_4.UI_Cross)
	elseif p47[1] == "Success" then
		local v_u_48 = v_u_25()
		local _ = string.split(v_u_48.FullName, " (")[1]
		v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.05, 0)
		for _, v49 in v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame:GetChildren() do
			if v49:IsA("ImageLabel") then
				v49:Destroy()
			end
		end
		local v50 = {}
		for v51, v52 in pairs(v_u_6.Gifts) do
			if v52.Crafted and string.find(v51, "Desk Calendar") then
				table.insert(v50, v51)
			end
		end
		for v53 = 1, 42 do
			local v54 = script.Icon:Clone()
			v54.Parent = v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame

				v54.Name = "Yes"
			else
				local v55 = v50[math.random(1, #v50)]
				v54.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v55].Image
			end
		end
		v_u_12.Visible = true
		v_u_5:Create(v_u_12.GiftFrame.TopFrame.RollFrame, TweenInfo.new(5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad), {
			["Position"] = UDim2.new(-13, 0, 0.05, 0)
		}):Play()
		for _, v_u_56 in v_u_13:GetDescendants() do
			if v_u_56:IsA("TextLabel") and v_u_48[v_u_56.Name] then
				task.spawn(function()
					-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_48, (copy) v_u_56
					local v57 = v_u_48[v_u_56.Name]

					for v59 = 1, string.len(v57) do
						local v60 = string.sub(v57, 1, v59)
						v_u_56.Text = v60 .. string.rep("?", string.len(v57) - string.len(v60))
						task.wait(v58)
					end
				end)
			end
		end
		task.spawn(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_17, (ref) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_13, (ref) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_48
			for _ = 1, 9 do
				if not v_u_17 then
					return
				end

				local v62 = v_u_13.TopFrame

				local v65 = {}
				local v66 = {}
				for v67, _ in v_u_6.Backdrops do

				end
				v66.BackgroundColor3 = v64[v65[math.random(1, #v65)]]
				v61:Create(v62, v63, v66):Play()

end
function TableFormat(p78, p79) -- name: TableFormat
	local v80 = {}
	for v81, v82 in ipairs(p78) do
		if v81 ~= p79 then
			table.insert(v80, v82)
		end
	end
	return v80
end

local function v_u_94(p_u_90) -- name: ItemFrame
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_87, (copy) v_u_46
	if p_u_90:GetAttribute("Delay") then
		task.wait(p_u_90:GetAttribute("Delay"))
		if p_u_90.Parent ~= v_u_7 then
			return
		end
	end
	if p_u_90:GetAttribute("Unique") then
		local v91 = p_u_90.Name
		if v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Price >= 10000 then
			local v_u_92 = script.UniqueFrame:Clone()
			v_u_92.Name = p_u_90.Name
			v_u_92.Txt.Text = v91
			v_u_92.Price.Text = "\240\159\146\160 " .. v_u_3.SimpleNumber(v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Price / 250)
			v_u_92.ImageLabel.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Image
			for _, v93 in v_u_92.Patterns:GetChildren() do
				v93.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. v_u_14[p_u_90:GetAttribute("Pattern")]
			end
			v_u_92.BackgroundColor3 = v_u_15[p_u_90:GetAttribute("Backdrop")]
			v_u_92.Count.Text = p_u_90:GetAttribute("Number")
			v_u_92.Parent = v_u_11
			v_u_92.Limited.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[v91].Limited
			v_u_92.Winter.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_90.Name].Winter
			v_u_92.Summer.Visible = v_u_6.Gifts[p_u_90.Name].Summer
			p_u_90.Destroying:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_92
				v_u_92:Destroy()
			end)
			v_u_92.Button.Activated:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_87, (ref) v_u_46, (copy) p_u_90
				if not v_u_87 then
					v_u_46(p_u_90)
				end
			end)
		end
	else
		return
	end
end

v_u_10.Button.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_87, (ref) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_10, (ref) v_u_86, (ref) v_u_83, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_4, (ref) v_u_19, (copy) v_u_115, (ref) v_u_84
	if v_u_87 then
		return
	elseif v_u_18 then
		return
	else
		task.spawn(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_18
			v_u_18 = true
			task.wait(1)
			v_u_18 = false
		end)
		if v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text == "Craft more" then
			v_u_10.FinalFrame.broken.Visible = false
			v_u_10.FinalFrame.hammer.Visible = true
			v_u_10.FinalFrame.anvil.Visible = true
			v_u_10.FinalFrame.safe.Visible = false
			v_u_10.info2.Text = "In case of failure, these gifts will be destroyed."
			v_u_10.Parent.Inventory.Visible = true
			v_u_10.Button.Txt.Text = "Craft"
			v_u_10.Button.Succ.Visible = true
			return
		elseif #v_u_86 < 1 and #v_u_86 > 4 then
			return
		else
			local v116 = {
				["Items"] = {},
				["FirstNumber"] = v_u_83
			}
			for _, v117 in ipairs(v_u_86) do
				local v118 = v116.Items
				local v119 = {
					["Name"] = v117.Name,
					["Number"] = v117:GetAttribute("Number")
				}
				table.insert(v118, v119)
			end
			local v120, v121 = v_u_2.Craft:InvokeServer(v116)
			if v120 then
				v_u_19 = task.spawn(v_u_115, v121)
				v_u_87 = true
				v_u_86 = {}

	local v56 = {}
	for v57, v58 in ipairs(p54) do

		end
	end

end

local v_u_38 = false
local function v_u_46(p39) -- name: ParseDateString
	local v40, v41, v42, v43, v44, v45 = p39:match("(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+):(%d+):(%d+)")
	return v40 and {
		["year"] = tonumber(v40),
		["month"] = tonumber(v41),
		["day"] = tonumber(v42),
		["hour"] = tonumber(v43),
		["min"] = tonumber(v44),
		["sec"] = tonumber(v45)
	} or nil
end
local function v_u_53(p47) -- name: GetTimeAgo
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_46
	if type(p47) == "string" then
		p47 = v_u_46(p47)
	end
	if type(p47) ~= "table" then
		return "Unknown time"
	end
	local v48 = os.time({
		["year"] = p47.year,
		["month"] = p47.month,
		["day"] = p47.day,
		["hour"] = p47.hour or 0,
		["min"] = p47.min or 0,
		["sec"] = p47.sec or 0
	})
	local v49 = os.time() - v48
	if v49 < 60 then
		return "Just now"
	end
	if v49 < 3600 then
		local v50 = v49 / 60
		return math.floor(v50) .. " min ago"
	end
	if v49 < 86400 then
		local v51 = v49 / 3600
		return math.floor(v51) .. " hours ago"
	end
	if v49 < 172800 then
		return "Yesterday"
	end
	local v52 = v49 / 86400
	return math.floor(v52) .. " days ago"
end
local function v_u_61(p54) -- name: GetLogTime
	if type(p54) == "string" then
		local v55, v56, v57, v58, v59, v60 = p54:match("(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+)/(%d+):(%d+):(%d+)")
		if not v55 then
			return os.time()
		end
		p54 = {
			["year"] = tonumber(v55),
			["month"] = tonumber(v56),
			["day"] = tonumber(v57),
			["hour"] = tonumber(v58),
			["min"] = tonumber(v59),
			["sec"] = tonumber(v60)
		}
	elseif type(p54) ~= "table" then
		return os.time()
	end
	return os.time({
		["year"] = p54.year,
		["month"] = p54.month,
		["day"] = p54.day,
		["hour"] = p54.hour or 0,
		["min"] = p54.min or 0,
		["sec"] = p54.sec or 0
	})
end

	local v64 = script.Parent.Upgrade
	local v65 = v_u_62.Value
	local v66 = v65 + 100
	local v67 = v_u_4.InventoryUpgradePrices[v66]
	if v67 then
		v64.Txt.Text = "<font color = \'#ffffff\'>" .. v65 .. "</font><font color = \'#cfcfcf\'> \226\134\146 </font><font color = \'#6dff5f\'>" .. v66 .. "</font> <font color = \'#ffffff\'>Slots</font>"
		v64.price.Text = v_u_34(v67) .. "\240\159\146\142"
		if v_u_63.Value < v67 then
			v64.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
		else
			v64.BackgroundTransparency = 0
		end
	else
		v64.Active = false
		v64.Txt.Text = "MAX"
		v64.price.Text = ""
		return
	end
end

local function v_u_23() -- name: PulsLoop

		until v_u_18 <= 0
		v_u_4:Create(v_u_12, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
			["Size"] = UDim2.new(0.55, 0, 0.55, 0)
		}):Play()
		task.wait(0.5)
		if v_u_18 <= 0 then
			v_u_4:Create(v_u_12, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut), {
				["Size"] = UDim2.new(0.45, 0, 0.45, 0)

		end
	end
end

function v_u_3.Rocket.OnClientInvoke(p33)
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_32, (copy) v_u_31, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_10
	if not v_u_17 then
		return true
	end
	v_u_32()
	task.spawn(v_u_31, "Rocket", false, true, p33)
	v_u_8.Txt.Text = "Play"
	if p33 then
		v_u_1.CreateSound(v_u_6.UI_Cross)
	else
		v_u_1.CreateSound(v_u_6.UI_Lose)
	end
	task.wait(2)
	v_u_17 = false
	v_u_10.Text = "x1.00"
	return true
end

function getRandomRotation(p83, p84) -- name: getRandomRotation
	local v85 = p83 > 0.75 and 0.75 or p83
	local v86 = math.random() * (p84 and v85 and v85 or 1 - v85)
	local v87 = p84 and v86 and v86 or 1 - v86
	local v88 = math.sqrt(v87)
	local v89 = math.asin(v88) * 2
	local v90 = p84 and 3.141592653589793 + v89 or 3.141592653589793 - v89
	local v91 = math.deg(v90)
	if math.random(1, 2) == 1 then
		v91 = 360 - v91
	end
	return v91
end

	v_u_1:Create(p9.Background, v_u_7, {
		["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1,
		["Position"] = nil,

	v_u_1:Create(p9.Background.TextLabel, v_u_7, {
		["TextTransparency"] = 1
	}):Play()
	local v10 = v_u_1:Create(p9.Background.TextLabel.UIStroke, v_u_7, {
		["Transparency"] = 1
	})
	v10:Play()
	v10.Completed:Wait()
	p9:Destroy()
end

end

	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_13, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_1
	if p_u_14 then
		local v_u_15 = v_u_6.Tasks[p_u_14.Name]
		if v_u_15 then
			local v_u_16 = script.Task:Clone()
			v_u_16.Heading.Text = v_u_15.Heading
			local v17 = v_u_15.SNOWFLAKES and "\226\157\132\239\184\143" or "\240\159\146\142"
			v_u_16.Reward.Text = "Reward: " .. v17 .. " " .. v_u_7.SimpleNumber(v_u_15.Reward)
			v_u_16.XPReward.Text = "XP: " .. "\240\159\148\181 " .. v_u_7.SimpleNumber(v_u_15.XPReward)
			local v18 = v_u_16.Icon

			v18.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. tostring(v19)
			if p_u_14:GetAttribute("Done") then
				v_u_16.Claim.Txt.Text = "Claimed"
				v_u_16.Claim.Txt.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0.792157, 0.792157, 0.792157)
			end
			local function v20() -- name: Count
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_16, (ref) v_u_7, (copy) p_u_14, (copy) v_u_15
				v_u_16.Count.Text = v_u_7.SimpleNumber(p_u_14.Value) .. "/" .. v_u_7.SimpleNumber(v_u_15.Goal)
				v_u_16.Progress.Bar.Size = UDim2.fromScale(p_u_14.Value / v_u_15.Goal, 1)
			end
			p_u_14.Changed:Connect(v20)
			v_u_16.Count.Text = v_u_7.SimpleNumber(p_u_14.Value) .. "/" .. v_u_7.SimpleNumber(v_u_15.Goal)
			v_u_16.Progress.Bar.Size = UDim2.fromScale(p_u_14.Value / v_u_15.Goal, 1)
			v_u_16.Claim.Activated:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13, (ref) v_u_8, (copy) p_u_14, (ref) v_u_7, (ref) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_16
				if v_u_13 then
					return
				else
					v_u_13 = true
					task.delay(0.3, function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13
						v_u_13 = false
					end)
					local v21, v22 = v_u_8.Tasks:InvokeServer("Claim", p_u_14)
					if v21 then

					end
				end
			end)
			p_u_14.Destroying:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_16
				v_u_16:Destroy()
			end)
			v_u_16.Parent = v_u_1:FindFirstChild(v_u_15.Duration)
		end
	else
		return
	end
end

v20.Activated:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_27, (ref) v_u_36, (copy) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_17, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_6, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_15, (copy) v_u_9
	if v_u_27 > 0 then
		return
	end
	if v_u_36 then
		return
	end
	v_u_36 = true
	task.delay(0.3, function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_36
		v_u_36 = false
	end)
	local v42 = {
		["Items"] = {},
		["Currency"] = {}
	}
	for _, v43 in ipairs(v_u_24.Items) do
		local v44 = v42.Items
		table.insert(v44, v43)
	end
	for _, v45 in ipairs(v_u_17:GetChildren()) do
		if v45:IsA("Frame") then
			local v46 = v45:GetAttribute("Amount") or 0
			if v46 >= 0 then
				v42.Currency[v45.Name] = v46
			end
		end
	end
	local v47 = false
	for _, v48 in pairs(v42.Currency) do
		if v48 > 0 then
			v47 = true
			break
		end
	end
	if #v42.Items > 0 or v47 then
		local v49, v50 = v_u_3.TradeClient:InvokeServer("AddToOffer", v42)
		if not v49 then
			v_u_5.Notify("ERROR", v50, v_u_6.UI_Error)
		end
		v_u_24.Items = {}
		for _, v51 in v_u_16:GetChildren() do
			if v51:IsA("Frame") then
				v51.Button:Destroy()
				if v51:FindFirstChild("Counter") then
					if v_u_10:FindFirstChild(v51.Name) then
						local v52 = v_u_10[v51.Name].Counter
						v52.Value = v52.Value + v51.Counter.Value
						v51:Destroy()
					else
						v51.Parent = v_u_10
					end
				else
					v51.Parent = v_u_10
				end
			end
		end
		for _, v53 in v_u_18:GetDescendants() do
			if v53.Name == "DisabledX" then
				v53:Destroy()
			end
		end
		for v54, v55 in pairs(v42.Currency) do
			local v56 = v_u_10.Parent.Currency:FindFirstChild(v54)
			if v55 > 0 and v55 <= v_u_22:FindFirstChild("_" .. v54).Value then
				if not v56 then
					v56 = script.CurrencyItem:Clone()
					v56.Name = v54
					v56.Parent = v_u_10.Parent.Currency
				end
				local v57 = v54 == "TONValue" and "\240\159\146\160" or (v54 == "GemsValue" and "\240\159\146\142" or "\226\173\144")
				v56.TextLabel.Text = v57 .. v_u_5.SimpleNumber(v55)
			elseif v56 then
				v56:Destroy()
			end
		end
		v_u_15.Visible = false
		v_u_9.Visible = true
	end
end)

v_u_3.TradeRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(p58, ...)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_10, (copy) v_u_11, (ref) v_u_35, (copy) v_u_14, (copy) v_u_9, (copy) v_u_24, (copy) v_u_18, (copy) v_u_16, (copy) v_u_21, (ref) v_u_37, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_23, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_5, (copy) v_u_25, (ref) v_u_27, (copy) v_u_8, (copy) v_u_6
	if p58 == "StartTrade" then
		local v59 = ...
		v_u_10.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, 0)
		v_u_11.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, 0)
		v_u_35 = false
		v_u_14.Txt.Text = "Confirm"

		v_u_9.Receiving.UIStroke.Color = Color3.new(0.305882, 0.298039, 0.309804)

		v_u_24.Currency = {
			["StarsValue"] = 0,
			["TONValue"] = 0,
			["GemsValue"] = 0
		}
		for _, v60 in v_u_11:GetChildren() do
			if v60:IsA("Frame") then
				v60:Destroy()
			end
		end
		for _, v61 in v_u_10:GetChildren() do
			if v61:IsA("Frame") and v61.Name ~= "Add" then
				v61:Destroy()
			end
		end
		for _, v62 in v_u_18.Scroll1:GetChildren() do

		end
		v_u_21.Stroke.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
		v_u_37 = "Default"
		v_u_7.Heading.Txt.Text = "Trade with " .. v59.Name
		for _, v_u_65 in v_u_23:GetChildren() do

					end)
					local v69 = v_u_24.Items

				v_u_75.Folder.Named.Text = v_u_66
				v_u_75.Folder.Stars.Text = "\226\173\144 " .. v_u_5.SimpleNumber(v_u_2.Gifts[v_u_66].Price)

									v_u_82:Destroy()

									v83.Value = v83.Value - 1

	elseif p58 == "UpdateCurrency" then
		for v97, v98 in pairs((...)) do

				local v99 = v97 == "TONValue" and "\240\159\146\160" or (v97 == "GemsValue" and "\240\159\146\142" or "\226\173\144")

				v107:Destroy()
			end
		end
		v_u_5.Notify("TRADE", "Something went wrong", v_u_6.UI_BLose)
	end
end)
